(Psalms 14:3) 
They have all turned away; together they have become worthless. There is no one who does good, not even one.

(Psalms 14:4) 
Their throat is an open tomb. With their tongues they practice deceit. The venom of asps is under their lips. Their mouth is full of cursing and bitterness.

(Psalms 14:5) 
Their feet are swift to shed blood. Destruction and misery are in their paths, and they have not known the way of peace. There is no fear of God before their eyes.

(Psalms 14:6) 
Will all those who work iniquity not know this—those who devour My people as if eating bread?

(Psalms 14:7) 
They have not called upon the Lord. There they trembled with fear where there was no fear.

(Psalms 14:8) 
For the Lord is with the generation of the just. You have confounded the counsel of the poor, because the Lord is his refuge.

(Psalms 14:9) 
Who will bring salvation for Israel from Sion? When the Lord restores the fortunes of His people, Jacob will rejoice and Israel will be glad.

(Psalms 15:1) 
Lord, who is worthy to dwell in Your holy presence, in Your tabernacle of worship? And who is worthy to rest on Your holy mountain of divine communion?

(Psalms 15:2) 
It is he who lives a blameless life and acts always with justice,

(Psalms 15:3) 
who speaks the truth from his heart,

(Psalms 15:4) 
who does not use his tongue to deceive others, and does not do evil to his neighbor, nor spreads slander or disgrace against those around him.

(Psalms 15:5) 
In his eyes, the wicked person is despised and considered nothing; but he honors those who revere the Lord. He keeps his promises to his neighbor, even if it brings him harm,

(Psalms 15:6) 
he does not lend his money at excessive interest to profit from the needy, nor does he accept bribes to harm an innocent person.

(Psalms 15:7) 
Whoever lives by these virtues will never be shaken from God's presence, for all eternity.

(Psalms 16:1) 
Lord, preserve me, for I have placed all my hope in you.

(Psalms 16:2) 
I said to the Lord, "You are my God; you have no need of anything I can do for you."

(Psalms 16:3) 
My entire delight is in the holy ones who live in His land.

(Psalms 16:4) 
Those who rush after other gods will only multiply their sorrows. I will not offer their blood sacrifices, nor will I even speak their names with my lips.

(Psalms 16:5) 
The Lord is my inheritance, the portion of my cup of blessing; it is you who will maintain my lot in life.

(Psalms 16:6) 
The measuring lines have marked out for me a beautiful land; indeed, my inheritance is truly magnificent.

(Psalms 16:7) 
I will bless the Lord, who has given me wisdom and understanding. Even in the depths of my being, my conscience guides me throughout the night.

(Psalms 16:8) 
I always keep the Lord before my eyes, for He is at my right hand, so I will never be shaken.

(Psalms 16:9) 
Because of this, my heart is full of joy, and my tongue sings praises. Moreover, my body will rest securely in hope.

(Psalms 16:10) 
For you will not abandon my soul to the realm of the dead, nor will you allow your Holy One to undergo decay.

(Psalms 16:11) 
You have revealed to me the path of life. You will fill me with joy through your presence; at your right hand there are eternal delights.

(Psalms 17:1) 
I will love you, O Lord, for you are my strength.

(Psalms 17:2) 
The Lord is my rock, my refuge, and my deliverer. My God is my helper, and I will place my hope in Him; He is my protector, the source of my strength and salvation, and my shield.

(Psalms 17:3) 
I will call upon the Lord with praises, and I will be saved from my enemies.

(Psalms 17:4) 
The sorrows of death surrounded me, and overwhelming floods of wickedness greatly troubled me.

(Psalms 17:5) 
The pains of the underworld surrounded me; the snares of death suddenly came upon me.

(Psalms 17:6) 
In my tribulation, I called upon the Lord, and to my God I cried for help. From His holy temple, He heard my voice, and my cry came into His hearing, before His very presence.

(Psalms 17:7) 
The earth was shaken and trembled; the mountains, too, were greatly disturbed and moved from their places, because He was angry with them.

(Psalms 17:8) 
Smoke ascended in His wrath, and fire flared from His presence; burning coals were ignited by Him.

(Psalms 17:9) 
He bent down the skies and descended; and dense darkness was beneath His feet.

(Psalms 17:10) 
And He ascended upon the cherubim, and flew; He flew upon the wings of the winds.

(Psalms 17:11) 
And He made darkness His hiding place; His dwelling surrounded Him, with dark water gathered in the clouds of the air.

(Psalms 17:12) 
Before the brightness of His presence, the clouds passed away, followed by hail and burning coals.

(Psalms 17:13) 
And the Lord thundered from the skies, and the Most High uttered His voice: hail and burning coals.

(Psalms 17:14) 
He sent out His arrows—His lightning bolts—and scattered them; He multiplied His flashes of lightning and threw them into confusion.

(Psalms 17:15) 
And the sources of the waters appeared, and the very foundations of the earth were revealed, at Your rebuke, O Lord, at the fierce blast of the breath of Your wrath.

(Psalms 17:16) 
He sent down from the highest place and took hold of me; He drew me out of overwhelming troubles, like many waters.

(Psalms 17:17) 
He rescued me from my most powerful enemies, and from those who hated me, because they had become too strong for me.

(Psalms 17:18) 
They confronted me on the day of my affliction; but the Lord became my protector.

(Psalms 17:19) 
And He brought me out into a place of freedom; He saved me, because He delighted in me.

(Psalms 17:20) 
And the Lord will reward me according to my righteousness; He will repay me according to the cleanness of my hands.

(Psalms 17:21) 
For I have kept the ways of the Lord, and have not acted wickedly against my God.

(Psalms 17:22) 
For all His judgments are before me, and I have not cast away His righteous decrees from me.

(Psalms 17:23) 
And I will be blameless before Him, and I will keep myself from my iniquity.

(Psalms 17:24) 
And the Lord will reward me according to my righteousness, and according to the cleanness of my hands in the sight of His eyes.

(Psalms 17:25) 
With the holy, You show Yourself holy; and with the innocent man, You show Yourself innocent.

(Psalms 17:26) 
And with the upright, You show Yourself upright; but with the perverse, You show Yourself contrary.

(Psalms 17:27) 
For You will save the humble people, and You will humble the proud.

(Psalms 17:28) 
For You, O Lord, light my lamp; my God, You enlighten my darkness.

(Psalms 17:29) 
For by You I shall be delivered from any attack; and by my God, I shall scale any wall.

(Psalms 17:30) 
My God, His way is perfect; the words of the Lord are refined by fire. He is a protector to all who hope in Him.

(Psalms 17:31) 
For who is God except the Lord? Or who is God except our God?

(Psalms 17:32) 
It is God who has girded me with strength, and has made my way perfect.

(Psalms 17:33) 
He made my feet like the feet of deer, and set me securely upon high places.

(Psalms 17:34) 
He trains my hands for battle; and You have strengthened my arms like a bow made of bronze.

(Psalms 17:35) 
And You have given me the shield of Your salvation; Your right hand has sustained me, and Your discipline has guided me completely, and Your instruction itself will teach me.

(Psalms 17:36) 
You have made a wide path for my steps beneath me, and my feet have not faltered.

(Psalms 17:37) 
I will pursue my enemies and overtake them; and I will not turn back until they are utterly defeated.

(Psalms 17:38) 
I will crush them, and they will not be able to stand; they will fall beneath my feet.

(Psalms 17:39) 
And You have girded me with strength for battle; You have made those who rise against me fall beneath me.

(Psalms 17:40) 
And You have made my enemies turn their backs and flee; You have utterly destroyed those who hated me.

(Psalms 17:41) 
They cried out, but there was no one to save them; they cried even to the Lord, but He did not hear them.

(Psalms 17:42) 
And I will crush them like dust before the wind; I will cast them out like the mud of the streets.

(Psalms 17:43) 
You will rescue me from the strife of the people; You will make me the head of nations. A people I have not known have served me.

(Psalms 17:44) 
At the mere hearing of my voice, they obeyed me. The sons of foreigners have lied to me.

(Psalms 17:45) 
The sons of foreigners have withered away and they have stumbled from their paths.

(Psalms 17:46) 
The Lord lives! And blessed be my God! And let the God of my salvation be greatly exalted!

(Psalms 17:47) 
It is God who grants me vengeance, and subdues peoples under me; He is my deliverer from wrathful nations.

(Psalms 17:48) 
And You will exalt me above those who rise against me; You will rescue me from the wicked man.

(Psalms 17:49) 
Therefore, I will give thanks to You, O Lord, among the nations, and I will sing a psalm to Your name.

(Psalms 17:50) 
He greatly delivers His king, and shows mercy to His Anointed One, David, and to his offspring forever and ever.

(Psalms 18:1) 
A Psalm of David, for the director.

(Psalms 18:2) 
The vast universe itself declares the glory of God. The very expanse of the sky proclaims the work of His hands.

(Psalms 18:3) 
Each day speaks to the next day, pouring out a message; each night points to the next night, revealing knowledge about God.

(Psalms 18:4) 
There are no spoken words, no human languages, and no voices that can explain it, yet their message is understood everywhere.

(Psalms 18:5) 
Their message travels across the entire earth; their words reach the very ends of the inhabited world. God has placed His dwelling of light in the sun.

(Psalms 18:6) 
And the sun, like a bridegroom leaving his wedding chamber, is joyful. It exults like a mighty man running his race.

(Psalms 18:7) 
Its rising begins at one end of the sky, and its journey carries it to the other end. Nothing can hide from its warmth and light.

(Psalms 18:8) 
The Law of the Lord is perfect and flawless, restoring people's souls. The testimony of the Lord is trustworthy, giving wisdom to those who are simple in heart.

(Psalms 18:9) 
The Lord's commands are just and right, bringing joy to one's heart. The commandment of the Lord is clear and bright, enlightening one's eyes.

(Psalms 18:10) 
The reverence for the Lord is holy, lasting for all generations. The judgments of the Lord are true, being righteous in every way.

(Psalms 18:11) 
These laws are more desirable than the finest gold and more valuable than many precious jewels. They are sweeter to taste than honey, even the fresh honey from the comb.

(Psalms 18:12) 
Your servant, O Lord, diligently guards and keeps these teachings. In the keeping of them, there is great reward and fulfillment.

(Psalms 18:13) 
Who can truly understand their own missteps and sins? Cleanse me, Lord, from my unintentional and hidden faults.

(Psalms 18:14) 
Keep your servant from sins committed out of pride or presumption. If these powerful sins do not gain control over me, then I will be without blemish, and I will be cleansed from the greatest of transgressions.

(Psalms 18:15) 
May the words that I speak and the thoughts of my heart always be pleasing in your sight, O Lord, my Helper and my Redeemer.

(Psalms 19:1) 
A Psalm of David, for the End.

(Psalms 19:2) 
The entire universe declares the glory of God. The atmosphere and all the works of His hands announce His greatness.

(Psalms 19:3) 
Day after day, creation pours forth knowledge of God; night after night, it reveals His wisdom.

(Psalms 19:4) 
No words are spoken, no verbal language is used, yet their voice, a silent testimony, is heard throughout the world.

(Psalms 19:5) 
Their silent witness has gone out into every land. Their message reaches the very ends of the inhabited world.

(Psalms 19:6) 
In the sky, God has set a dwelling place for the sun. And the sun itself, like a bridegroom coming forth from his bridal chamber,

(Psalms 19:7) 
It rejoices like a mighty hero ready to run its course. Its going forth is from one end of the sky,

(Psalms 19:8) 
And its circuit reaches all the way to the other end of the sky. Nothing is hidden from its heat.

(Psalms 19:9) 
The law of the Lord is perfect; it restores the soul. The testimony of the Lord is trustworthy; it gives wisdom to the simple.

(Psalms 19:10) 
The statutes of the Lord are right; they bring joy to the heart. The commandment of the Lord is clear; it enlightens the eyes.

(Psalms 19:11) 
The fear of the Lord is holy; it endures forever. The judgments of the Lord are true and altogether righteous.

(Psalms 19:12) 
They are more desirable than gold, than much fine gold, and sweeter than honey, even honeycomb.

(Psalms 19:13) 
Moreover, your servant keeps them; in keeping them, there is great reward.

(Psalms 19:14) 
Who can discern his own hidden faults? Cleanse me from those sins I do not know.

(Psalms 19:15) 
Keep your servant also from sins of pride and presumption; do not let them gain dominion over me. Then I shall be blameless and innocent of great transgression.

(Psalms 19:16) 
May the words of my mouth and the meditation of my heart be always pleasing in Your sight,

(Psalms 19:17) 
O Lord, my strength and my redeemer.

(Psalms 20:1) 
For the conductor, a Psalm of David.

(Psalms 20:2) 
May the Lord hear you in your time of trouble; may the name of the God of Jacob protect you.

(Psalms 20:3) 
May He send you help from His holy dwelling place and defend you from Zion.

(Psalms 20:4) 
May He remember all your sacrifices, and may He accept your burnt offering as pleasing.

(Psalms 20:5) 
May He grant you what your heart desires and confirm all your plans.

(Psalms 20:6) 
We will rejoice in the salvation He brings you, and in the name of our God, we will triumph.

(Psalms 20:7) 
May the Lord fulfill all your requests. Now I know that the Lord has saved His anointed one, the king.

(Psalms 20:8) 
He will hear him from His holy dwelling place, through the omnipotent saving power of His right hand.

(Psalms 20:9) 
Some nations trust in their chariots, and some in their horses, but we will call upon the name of the Lord our God.

(Psalms 20:10) 
They were brought down and have fallen, but we have risen and stand firm.

(Psalms 20:11) 
Lord, save the king, and hear us when we call upon You.

(Psalms 21:1) 
My God, my God, look upon me. Why have You forsaken me? My words, even those crying out in my deep distress because of my sins, feel far from bringing me salvation.

(Psalms 21:2) 
My God, I cry out to You all day long, yet You do not answer me. I cry out through the night, and my constant prayer is not foolishness.

(Psalms 21:3) 
But You, O God, dwell among Your holy ones, and You are the very object of Israel's praise.

(Psalms 21:4) 
Our fathers hoped in You. They hoped, and You rescued them from their troubles.

(Psalms 21:5) 
They cried out to You, and they found salvation. They placed their hope in You, and they were never put to shame.

(Psalms 21:6) 
But I feel like a mere worm, not even a true man. I have become a disgrace among all men, and I am despised by the common people.

(Psalms 21:7) 
All who saw me mocked me openly. They spoke contemptuously and shook their heads at me in scorn.

(Psalms 21:8) 
They mock me, saying: "He trusted in the Lord, so let the Lord rescue him! Let the Lord save him, if the Lord truly delights in him!"

(Psalms 21:9) 
For it was You, O God, who brought me safely from my mother's womb. My hope in You began when I was still at my mother's breast.

(Psalms 21:10) 
I was entrusted to Your care from the moment I left my mother's womb. From my very birth, You have been my God.

(Psalms 21:11) 
Do not stay far from me now, because trouble is very near, and there is no one else to help me.

(Psalms 21:12) 
Many strong young bulls surround me. Powerful and well-fed enemies have pressed in on me from every side.

(Psalms 21:13) 
They open their mouths wide against me, like a ravenous, roaring lion seeking to tear its prey.

(Psalms 21:14) 
I am poured out like water, completely without strength. All my bones are disjointed and out of place. My heart has become like wax melting within me, in the very center of my being.

(Psalms 21:15) 
My strength is dried up like a broken piece of pottery, and my tongue sticks to the roof of my mouth. You have brought me down to the dust of death, where all life ends.

(Psalms 21:16) 
Many wild dogs surround me. A band of wicked men have surrounded me, pressing in on all sides. They have pierced my hands and my feet.

(Psalms 21:17) 
They count every one of my bones, as if I am a skeleton exposed. They stare at me, observing me with cruel satisfaction.

(Psalms 21:18) 
They divide my clothing among themselves, and for my main tunic, they cast lots to decide who will take it.

(Psalms 21:19) 
But You, O Lord, do not hold back Your help from me. Look to my defense, and come quickly to my aid!

(Psalms 21:20) 
Rescue my life, O God, from the sword. Deliver my precious, unique life from the power of these wild dogs!

(Psalms 21:21) 
Save me from the mouth of the roaring lion! And deliver my humble and afflicted soul from the horns of those wild oxen!

(Psalms 21:22) 
I will proclaim Your holy name to my brethren, those who believe in You. Within the assembly of Your Church, I will praise You with joyful song.

(Psalms 21:23) 
All of you who revere the Lord, praise Him! All descendants of Jacob, who form Your people, give Him glory!

(Psalms 21:24) 
Let all the people of Israel revere Him with deep respect, for He did not scorn nor despise the humble prayer of one who was suffering. He did not turn His face away from me, and when I cried out to Him, He listened and heard my plea.

(Psalms 21:25) 
My praise for You will be offered in the great assembly of the faithful. I will fulfill the promises I made to You in the presence of all who revere You.

(Psalms 21:26) 
Those who have suffered and are spiritually poor will eat of Your bounty and be satisfied. And those who earnestly seek the Lord will praise Him. Their hearts will live on, full of joy, for all eternity.

(Psalms 21:27) 
All the nations and peoples throughout the whole earth will remember God and turn back to the Lord. And all the families of the Gentiles will worship before Him, acknowledging His supreme authority.

(Psalms 21:28) 
For the entire kingdom of the universe belongs to the Lord, and He alone will reign over all the nations and peoples.

(Psalms 21:29) 
Even those who are rich and powerful on earth have eaten of His bounty and will bow down to worship Him. All who are destined to return to the earth in death will bow before His presence.

(Psalms 21:30) 
My soul, my very being, will live for Him. And my descendants, my spiritual children, will serve Him faithfully.

(Psalms 21:31) 
A generation yet to be born will be told about the Lord and His wondrous deeds. And the very heavens will proclaim His righteousness to a new people who will be born, a people whom the Lord Himself has brought into being.

(Psalms 22:1) 
The Lord is my shepherd, and I will lack nothing.

(Psalms 22:2) 
He has settled me in fields full of fresh, green grass. He has led me up alongside waters of refreshment.

(Psalms 22:3) 
He has brought my soul back to Him. He has guided me along paths of righteousness, all for the sake of His name.

(Psalms 22:4) 
Even if I walk through the darkest valley of the shadow of death, I will not fear any evil, because You are with me. Your staff and Your rod, these have comforted me.

(Psalms 22:5) 
You have prepared a table for me in Your sight, even against those who trouble me. You have anointed my head with oil, and how glorious is my overflowing cup!

(Psalms 22:6) 
And Your mercy will follow me all the days of my life; and I will dwell in the house of the Lord for all eternity.

(Psalms 23:1) 
A Psalm of David. The Lord shepherds me, and I will want for nothing.

(Psalms 23:2) 
He settles me in green pastures. He guides me beside restful waters.

(Psalms 23:3) 
He restores my soul. He leads me on paths of righteousness for the glory of His name.

(Psalms 23:4) 
Even though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil, for You are with me. Your rod and Your staff—these comfort me.

(Psalms 23:5) 
You prepare a table before me in the presence of my enemies. You anoint my head with oil; my cup overflows with Your blessings.

(Psalms 23:6) 
And Your mercy will follow me all the days of my life, so that I may dwell in the house of the Lord for all eternity.

(Psalms 24:1) 
The Lord owns the earth and everything in it; He owns the entire world and all who live there.

(Psalms 24:2) 
For He himself established it upon the seas and secured it upon the rivers.

(Psalms 24:3) 
Who is worthy to ascend to the Lord's mountain? Or who is worthy to stand in His holy place?

(Psalms 24:4) 
He who has clean hands and a pure heart, who has not set his soul on worthless things, nor sworn deceitfully to his neighbor.

(Psalms 24:5) 
He will receive a blessing from the Lord and mercy from God, his Savior.

(Psalms 24:6) 
This is the generation of those who seek Him, of those who seek the face of the God of Jacob—the God of His chosen people.

(Psalms 24:7) 
Lift up your gates, you princes! And be lifted up, you eternal gates, so that the King of glory may enter.

(Psalms 24:8) 
Who is this King of glory? The Lord, strong and mighty; the Lord, powerful in battle.

(Psalms 24:9) 
Lift up your gates, you princes! And be lifted up, you eternal gates, so that the King of glory may enter.

(Psalms 24:10) 
Who is this King of glory? The Lord of all heavenly powers—He Himself is the King of glory.

(Psalms 25:1) 
To you, my Lord, I lift up my entire self.

(Psalms 25:2) 
My God, I trust completely in You. Do not let me be put to shame. Do not let my enemies mock me.

(Psalms 25:3) 
For all those who wait patiently on You will not be put to shame. Rather, let those who act with injustice and without cause be put to shame.

(Psalms 25:4) 
My Lord, show me your ways, and teach me Your paths of righteousness.

(Psalms 25:5) 
Guide me in Your truth and teach me, for You are God, my Savior, and I have waited on You all day long.

(Psalms 25:6) 
My Lord, remember Your tender mercies and Your loving-kindnesses, which have been from the beginning of time.

(Psalms 25:7) 
Do not remember the sins of my youth and my ignorances. According to Your great mercy, remember me, because of Your goodness, my Lord.

(Psalms 25:8) 
The Lord is good and righteous. Because of this, He will give His law to those who stray from His path.

(Psalms 25:9) 
He will guide the humble in judgment; He will teach the meek His ways.

(Psalms 25:10) 
All the ways of the Lord are mercy and truth to those who seek out His covenant and His testimonies.

(Psalms 25:11) 
For the sake of Your own name, My Lord, be merciful and forgive my sin, for it is indeed great.

(Psalms 25:12) 
Who is the person who truly fears the Lord? God establishes a law for him on the path which he has chosen.

(Psalms 25:13) 
His soul will dwell in prosperity, and his children's children will inherit the earth.

(Psalms 25:14) 
The Lord is a strong fortress for those who fear Him. He makes His covenant known to them.

(Psalms 25:15) 
My eyes are always fixed on the Lord, for He himself will free my feet from the trap.

(Psalms 25:16) 
Look upon me and have mercy on me, for I am lonely and poor.

(Psalms 25:17) 
The troubles of my heart have multiplied; deliver me from my necessities.

(Psalms 25:18) 
Look upon my lowliness and my toil, and forgive all my sins.

(Psalms 25:19) 
Look at my enemies, for they have multiplied, and they hate me with an unjust hatred.

(Psalms 25:20) 
Protect my life and rescue me. I will not be put to shame, for I have placed my hope in You.

(Psalms 25:21) 
Let innocence and uprightness preserve me, because I have waited patiently for You, my Lord.

(Psalms 25:22) 
O God, deliver the people of Israel from all their troubles.

(Psalms 26:1) 
The Lord is the source of my understanding, and He is my salvation—so whom shall I fear? The Lord is the protector of my entire life—so before whom shall I tremble?

(Psalms 26:2) 
When evil people approached to utterly destroy me, my very enemies who troubled me were themselves weakened and fell down.

(Psalms 26:3) 
If an entire army camps against me, my heart will not be afraid. If a battle rises up against me, even in this situation, I will place my hope in God.

(Psalms 26:4) 
I have asked one thing from the Lord, and this I will diligently seek: that I may dwell in the presence of the Lord all the days of my life, that I may perceive the will of the Lord, and that I may seek Him in His holy temple.

(Psalms 26:5) 
For He will conceal me within His sacred dwelling. In the day of evils, He will protect me in the secret place of His tent. He will lift me high upon a secure rock.

(Psalms 26:6) 
And now, He has raised my head above my enemies, granting me victory. I have walked around His dwelling, and I have offered in His tent a sacrifice of exultation and joy. I will sing and give praise to the Lord.

(Psalms 26:7) 
Hear, O Lord, my voice with which I have cried out to You. Show me Your mercy, and hear my prayer.

(Psalms 26:8) 
My heart has said to You, 'My whole being has sought You.' Your face, O Lord, I will continually seek.

(Psalms 26:9) 
Do not turn Your face away from me. Do not, in Your anger, turn away from Your servant. Be my helper; do not abandon me, nor despise me, O God, my Savior.

(Psalms 26:10) 
Even if my father and my mother were to abandon me, the Lord would nonetheless take me up and care for me.

(Psalms 26:11) 
Teach me Your way, O Lord. Guide me along a straight path because of my enemies, so I do not falter.

(Psalms 26:12) 
Do not deliver me over to the malicious desires of those who trouble me. For unjust witnesses have risen up against me, and their wickedness has proven to be a lie against itself.

(Psalms 26:13) 
I am confident that I shall see the good things of the Lord while I am still in the land of the living—that is, in this earthly life.

(Psalms 26:14) 
Wait for the Lord; be courageous, and let your heart be strengthened. Yes, continue to wait for the Lord.

(Psalms 27:1) 
From David. The Lord is my light, illuminating my path and my salvation; whom should I fear? The Lord protects my life; whom should I dread or be afraid of?

(Psalms 27:2) 
When evil people came against me, intent on destroying me, my enemies who troubled me, they stumbled and fell. They grew weak and collapsed.

(Psalms 27:3) 
Even if an army sets up camp against me, my heart will not be afraid. Even if a war breaks out against me, I will still hope in the Lord and trust Him.

(Psalms 27:4) 
I have asked the Lord for one thing, and this is what I will always seek: to live in the presence of the Lord all the days of my life. This is so I may contemplate the beauty of the Lord and always be near His holy temple.

(Psalms 27:5) 
Because in times of trouble, He will hide me in His sacred dwelling place, His tabernacle. He will protect me in the secret depths of His presence.

(Psalms 27:6) 
He has set me high upon a solid rock. And now, He has raised my head above all my enemies, giving me victory and honor.

(Psalms 27:7) 
I will circle His tabernacle in joyful procession, and there I will offer a sacrifice of praise with shouts of joy. I will sing and make music to the Lord, giving Him honor.

(Psalms 27:8) 
Hear my voice, O Lord, when I call out to You in prayer. Have mercy on me, and listen to my pleas.

(Psalms 27:9) 
My heart spoke to You, saying, 'My entire being seeks You out.' I will diligently seek Your presence, O Lord.

(Psalms 27:10) 
Do not turn Your face away from me, and do not reject Your servant in anger. Be my helper. Do not abandon me, nor look down upon me, O God, my Savior and the source of my salvation.

(Psalms 27:11) 
Even if my father and my mother were to abandon me, the Lord Himself would take me in and care for me.

(Psalms 27:12) 
Teach me Your way, O Lord. Guide me on a straight and righteous path because of those who watch to harm me.

(Psalms 27:13) 
Do not give me over to the malicious desires of those who trouble me. For false witnesses have risen up against me, and their wickedness has proven itself to be a lie.

(Psalms 27:14) 
I firmly believe that I will see the goodness of the Lord here, in this life, in the land of the living.

(Psalms 27:15) 
Wait patiently for the Lord to act. Be strong and courageous, and let your heart take courage. Yes, wait patiently for the Lord.

(Psalms 28:1) 
A Psalm of David. Offer to the Lord, you divine beings. Offer to the Lord, you mighty ones. Offer to the Lord His glory and honor.

(Psalms 28:2) 
Offer to the Lord glory in His name. Worship the Lord in His sacred court.

(Psalms 28:3) 
The voice of the Lord echoes over the waters. The God of Majesty has thundered. The Lord rules over all the mighty waters.

(Psalms 28:4) 
The voice of the Lord is filled with power. The voice of the Lord is majestic.

(Psalms 28:5) 
The voice of the Lord shatters the cedar trees. The Lord shatters the cedars of Lebanon.

(Psalms 28:6) 
He makes them, the cedars, leap like a calf from Lebanon. And He makes His beloved land leap like a young wild ox.

(Psalms 28:7) 
The voice of the Lord strikes forth flashes of fire.

(Psalms 28:8) 
The voice of the Lord shakes the desert. The Lord makes the desert of Kadesh tremble.

(Psalms 28:9) 
The voice of the Lord causes the deer to give birth, and strips bare the forests. In His sacred temple, everyone will declare His glory.

(Psalms 28:10) 
The Lord presides over the floodwaters. And the Lord will reign as king forever.

(Psalms 28:11) 
The Lord will give strength to His people. The Lord will bless His people with peace.

(Psalms 29:1) 
Offer to the Lord, O celestial beings; offer to the Lord, O powerful ones, your strength.

(Psalms 29:2) 
Offer to the Lord glory and honor; offer to the Lord the glory of His name. Worship the Lord in His holy court.

(Psalms 29:3) 
The voice of the Lord is over the vast waters; the God of majesty has thundered; the Lord is enthroned over the mighty waters.

(Psalms 29:4) 
The voice of the Lord is full of power; the voice of the Lord is full of majesty.

(Psalms 29:5) 
The voice of the Lord breaks apart the cedars; indeed, the Lord breaks the cedars of Lebanon.

(Psalms 29:6) 
He makes them leap like a young bull of Lebanon, and the beloved land itself skips like a young wild ox.

(Psalms 29:7) 
The voice of the Lord strikes forth bolts of lightning.

(Psalms 29:8) 
The voice of the Lord shakes the desert; the Lord causes the desert of Kadesh to tremble.

(Psalms 29:9) 
The voice of the Lord makes the hinds give birth prematurely, and strips bare the dense forests. And in His temple, everyone will proclaim His glory.

(Psalms 29:10) 
The Lord presided over the great flood; and the Lord will reign as King forever.

(Psalms 29:11) 
The Lord will give strength to His people; the Lord will bless His people with true peace.

(Psalms 30:1) 
For the end. A Psalm of David.

(Psalms 30:2) 
In You, O Lord, I have placed my hope. I will never be confounded or disgraced. By Your justice, set me free.

(Psalms 30:3) 
Listen closely to me, incline Your ear. Hurry to rescue me. Be my protecting God, my safe home, to deliver me.

(Psalms 30:4) 
For You are my strength and my safe place. And for the glory of Your Name, You will lead me and provide for me.

(Psalms 30:5) 
You will pull me out of this hidden trap that they set for me, for You are my guardian.

(Psalms 30:6) 
Into Your hands I entrust my very life. You have saved me, O Lord, God who is truth itself.

(Psalms 30:7) 
You despise those who foolishly worship worthless things.

(Psalms 30:8) 
But I, for my part, have put my trust in the Lord.

(Psalms 30:9) 
I will rejoice and be glad in Your mercy. For You have seen my lowliness, You have delivered my life from desperate distress.

(Psalms 30:10) 
You did not let my enemies trap me. You have given me freedom and a safe place to stand.

(Psalms 30:11) 
Have mercy on me, O Lord, for I am in distress. My sight is dim from grief, my soul is consumed by sorrow, and my very body wastes away.

(Psalms 30:12) 
My life is spent in misery, my years consumed by groans. My strength fails because of my affliction, and my bones are wasting away.

(Psalms 30:13) 
Because of all my enemies, I am mocked and shamed. Even my neighbors and my friends are now afraid of me. Everyone who sees me on the street runs away.

(Psalms 30:14) 
I am forgotten, as if I were dead and gone from their memory. I am like a broken, useless pot.

(Psalms 30:15) 
I hear the slanders of many who gather around me. As they conspire against me together, they plan to take my life.

(Psalms 30:16) 
But I, for my part, have trusted in You, O Lord. I declare: 'You are my God!'

(Psalms 30:17) 
My destiny is in Your hands. Rescue me from the power of my enemies and from those who pursue me.

(Psalms 30:18) 
Let Your face shine with favor upon Your servant. Save me because of Your steadfast love.

(Psalms 30:19) 
O Lord, I will not be put to shame, for I have called upon Your name. Let the wicked be disgraced and cast down into the realm of the dead.

(Psalms 30:20) 
Let their lying lips be silenced, those who speak evil against the righteous with arrogance and contempt.

(Psalms 30:21) 
How immense is Your goodness, O Lord! You store it up for those who reverence You. You lavish it upon those who trust in You, for all people to see.

(Psalms 30:22) 
You keep them safe in Your presence, away from human plotting. You shield them in Your sanctuary from slanderous words.

(Psalms 30:23) 
Blessed be the Lord, for He has wondrously shown His faithful love to me as if in a strong, safe city.

(Psalms 30:24) 
But I, in my panic and despair, thought: 'I am utterly cut off from Your sight.' Yet You heard my plea when I cried out to You.

(Psalms 30:25) 
Love the Lord, all His holy ones! For the Lord preserves the faithful, but harshly punishes those who act with arrogance.

(Psalms 30:26) 
Be strong and courageous, and let your hearts be strengthened, all of you who place your hope in the Lord.

(Psalms 31:1) 
Blessed are those whose wicked deeds have been forgiven, and whose personal sins have been completely covered by God's mercy.

(Psalms 31:2) 
Blessed is the person to whom the Lord does not hold their sin against them, and in whose spirit there is no deceit, no hidden guilt.

(Psalms 31:3) 
For when I kept silent about my sin and would not confess it, my strength wasted away. My very bones grew weak as I groaned and cried out all day long.

(Psalms 31:4) 
For day and night, Your heavy hand of correction was upon me. I was completely exhausted and overwhelmed, like one pierced by a thorn, in my deep distress.

(Psalms 31:5) 
I made my transgression known to You. And I did not hide my wrongdoing. I said to myself, "I will confess my wrongdoing against myself to the Lord." And You, O Lord, then forgave the wickedness of my sin.

(Psalms 31:6) 
For this reason, every faithful one will pray to You at the proper time of their need. Surely, even when great floods of overwhelming troubles come upon them, these troubles will not come near or overwhelm the faithful.

(Psalms 31:7) 
You are my safe refuge from the troubles that surround me. You are my joy and my song of triumph. Deliver me from those who would entrap me.

(Psalms 31:8) 
I will give you understanding and insight, says the Lord. And I will teach you the way you should walk. My eyes will be firmly fixed on you, guiding and watching over you.

(Psalms 31:9) 
Do not be like a horse or a mule, which have no understanding. Their mouths must be restrained with a bit and a bridle; otherwise, they will not come near to you, they will stray.

(Psalms 31:10) 
Many are the scourges and punishments for the wicked who refuse God. But mercy will surround those who put their hope and trust in the Lord.

(Psalms 31:11) 
Rejoice in the Lord! And exult with joy, you righteous ones! And glory in Him, all you who are upright in heart!

(Psalms 32:1) 
Rejoice and be joyful, you who are righteous, in the Lord; praise is fitting for those whose hearts are pure.

(Psalms 32:2) 
Give thanks to the Lord with a lyre; sing praises to Him with a ten-stringed harp.

(Psalms 32:3) 
Sing a new song to Him; make music skillfully to Him with loud shouts of joy.

(Psalms 32:4) 
For the word of the Lord is right and true, and all of His works are done in faithfulness and truth.

(Psalms 32:5) 
The Lord loves mercy and justice; the earth is full of the Lord's merciful love.

(Psalms 32:6) 
By the word of the Lord, the universe was made firm, and by the breath of His mouth, all its power and forces came into being.

(Psalms 32:7) 
He gathers the waters of the sea as if into a waterskin; He places the deep oceans into His storehouses.

(Psalms 32:8) 
Let all the earth fear the Lord; let all who inhabit the world stand in awe and reverence of Him.

(Psalms 32:9) 
For He spoke, and it came into being; He commanded, and it was created.

(Psalms 32:10) 
The Lord brings to nothing the plans of the nations; He frustrates the intentions of the peoples, and He rejects the schemes of rulers.

(Psalms 32:11) 
But the plan of the Lord stands firm forever; the intentions of His heart endure from generation to generation.

(Psalms 32:12) 
Blessed is the nation whose God is the Lord; blessed are the people He has chosen for His own inheritance.

(Psalms 32:13) 
From the created sky, the Lord looked down; He saw all the children of humankind.

(Psalms 32:14) 
From His prepared dwelling, He looked down upon all those who inhabit the earth.

(Psalms 32:15) 
He who formed each of their hearts individually; He who understands all of their works.

(Psalms 32:16) 
A king is not saved by a great army; nor is a warrior rescued by his great strength.

(Psalms 32:17) 
A war-horse is a deceptive means of salvation; nor will it deliver anyone by its abundant power.

(Psalms 32:18) 
Behold, the eyes of the Lord are upon those who fear Him; and upon those who hope in His merciful love.

(Psalms 32:19) 
He watches over them to deliver their souls from death; and to keep them alive during times of famine.

(Psalms 32:20) 
Our soul waits patiently for the Lord; for He is our helper and our protector.

(Psalms 32:21) 
For in Him our heart will rejoice; and in His holy name we will place our hope.

(Psalms 32:22) 
Let Your merciful love, O Lord, be upon us; just as we have hoped in You.

(Psalms 33:1) 
Rejoice in the Lord, you who are righteous; praise is fitting for those whose hearts are upright.

(Psalms 33:2) 
Give thanks to the Lord with the zither; sing to Him with a ten-stringed psaltery.

(Psalms 33:3) 
Sing to Him a new song; play skillfully and shout for joy to Him.

(Psalms 33:4) 
Because the word of the Lord is right and true, and all His works are done with faithfulness.

(Psalms 33:5) 
He loves mercy and justice; the whole earth is filled with the Lord's mercy and unfailing love.

(Psalms 33:6) 
By the word of the Lord, the universe was established, and by the breath of His mouth, all its power came into being.

(Psalms 33:7) 
He gathered the waters of the sea like a wineskin, storing the deep waters in His hidden treasuries.

(Psalms 33:8) 
Let all the earth fear the Lord; let all who live in the world tremble before Him.

(Psalms 33:9) 
For He spoke, and it came to be; He commanded, and it was created and stood firm.

(Psalms 33:10) 
The Lord frustrates the plans of the nations; He thwarts the schemes of the peoples and rejects the counsels of their leaders.

(Psalms 33:11) 
But the Lord's plan stands forever; the intentions of His heart endure from generation to generation.

(Psalms 33:12) 
Blessed is the nation whose God is the Lord; blessed are the people He has chosen as His own inheritance.

(Psalms 33:13) 
From the universe, the Lord looked down; He saw all the children of mankind.

(Psalms 33:14) 
From His established dwelling place, He looked upon all who live on the earth.

(Psalms 33:15) 
He who formed each of their hearts individually; He who understands all their works and actions.

(Psalms 33:16) 
A king is not saved by his great army, nor is a warrior rescued by his vast strength.

(Psalms 33:17) 
A warhorse is a deceitful hope for victory; despite its great power, it cannot deliver salvation.

(Psalms 33:18) 
Behold, the eyes of the Lord are upon those who fear Him; upon those who hope in His mercy.

(Psalms 33:19) 
He watches over them to rescue their souls from death and to sustain them during famine.

(Psalms 33:20) 
Our soul waits patiently for the Lord, for He is our helper and our shield.

(Psalms 33:21) 
Because in Him our heart will rejoice, and we have trusted in His holy Name.

(Psalms 33:22) 
Let Your mercy, O Lord, be upon us, just as we have hoped in You.

(Psalms 34:1) 
This is a psalm of David. He wrote it when he pretended to be insane in front of King Abimelech, who then sent him away.

(Psalms 34:2) 
I will give thanks to the Lord at all times and in every circumstance; His praise will always be upon my lips.

(Psalms 34:3) 
My soul will praise the Lord, finding its glory in Him. Let all those who are humble and gentle hear this, and let them rejoice.

(Psalms 34:4) 
Join with me in praising the Lord; let us together lift up His holy name.

(Psalms 34:5) 
I sought the Lord in my distress, and He heard my prayer; He rescued me from every single one of my troubles.

(Psalms 34:6) 
Come close to God, and He will give you light and understanding; then you will not be ashamed or disappointed.

(Psalms 34:7) 
This poor man cried out to God for help, and the Lord heard him; He saved him from all of his afflictions.

(Psalms 34:8) 
The angel of the Lord camps around those who revere Him, protecting them; and He rescues them from danger.

(Psalms 34:9) 
Experience for yourselves and see how good the Lord is; blessed is the man who trusts in Him.

(Psalms 34:10) 
Respect and revere the Lord, all you His holy ones, because those who truly fear Him lack nothing good.

(Psalms 34:11) 
Even the wealthy often suffer want and hunger; but those who diligently seek the Lord will never lack any good thing.

(Psalms 34:12) 
Come, my children, and listen to me; I will teach you what it means to truly revere the Lord.

(Psalms 34:13) 
Who is the man who desires true life, and longs to see many good days?

(Psalms 34:14) 
Keep your tongue from speaking evil, and your lips from uttering deceitful words.

(Psalms 34:15) 
Turn away from doing evil, and instead do what is good; seek peace actively, and follow after it.

(Psalms 34:16) 
The Lord's gaze is upon those who are righteous, and His ears are open to their prayers.

(Psalms 34:17) 
But the Lord is set against those who do evil, intending to erase their memory from the face of the earth.

(Psalms 34:18) 
When the righteous cry out to Him, the Lord hears them; and He delivers them from all their troubles.

(Psalms 34:19) 
The Lord is close to those whose hearts are broken and contrite; He saves those who are humble in spirit.

(Psalms 34:20) 
The righteous will experience many hardships; yet, from all these, the Lord will deliver them.

(Psalms 34:21) 
The Lord protects every part of their being, down to their very bones; not one of them will be broken.

(Psalms 34:22) 
The death of sinners is a terrible end; and those who hate the righteous will be punished for their offenses.

(Psalms 34:23) 
The Lord will redeem the souls of His servants; and none of those who place their hope in Him will be condemned or found guilty.

(Psalms 35:1) 
For the end. A Psalm of David. Judge, Lord, those who would harm me; fight those who attack me.

(Psalms 35:2) 
Pick up your weapons and your shield, and come to help me!

(Psalms 35:3) 
Draw your sword, and close in on those who are chasing me. Say to my soul, “I am your salvation!”

(Psalms 35:4) 
Let those who seek to destroy my life be shamed and disgraced. Let those who plot evil against me be turned back and confused.

(Psalms 35:5) 
Let them become like dust before the wind, and let the angel of the Lord oppress them.

(Psalms 35:6) 
Let their path be dark and slippery, and let the angel of the Lord pursue them.

(Psalms 35:7) 
For they have hidden the pitfall of their net for me without cause, and they have attacked my soul without cause.

(Psalms 35:8) 
Let destruction come upon him unexpectedly; let the trap he set catch him, and let him fall into it.

(Psalms 35:9) 
Then my soul will rejoice in the Lord, and delight in His salvation.

(Psalms 35:10) 
All my bones will say, “Lord, who is like you?” You rescue the poor from the hands of the strong, and the needy from those who would plunder them.

(Psalms 35:11) 
Those who accuse me falsely rise up; they question me about things I do not know.

(Psalms 35:12) 
They repay me evil for good, and cause me to suffer. 

(Psalms 35:13) 
But as for me, when they were attacking me, I put on sackcloth,

(Psalms 35:14) 
I humbled my soul with fasting, and my prayer will be returned to my own heart.

(Psalms 35:15) 
I acted as if they were my neighbor and brother; I mourned as if I was grieving and humbled.

(Psalms 35:16) 
But they rejoiced against me and gathered together; they gathered against me to bring trouble, and I did not know it.

(Psalms 35:17) 
They were scattered, they did not relent; they gnashed their teeth against me.

(Psalms 35:18) 
Lord, when will you look? Rescue my soul from their wickedness, from these lions, my life.

(Psalms 35:19) 
I will give thanks to you in the great assembly; I will praise you among the great people.

(Psalms 35:20) 
Let not those who are wrongly attacking me rejoice over me; they hate me without cause, and they wink their eyes.

(Psalms 35:21) 
For they do not speak of peace to me, but they speak of treachery, devising deceit in their hearts.

(Psalms 35:22) 
They said, “Aha, aha, our eyes have seen what we wanted!

(Psalms 35:23) 
You have seen this, Lord, do not be silent; Lord, do not withdraw from me!

(Psalms 35:24) 
Arise and awake for my vindication, for my cause, O my God and my Lord.

(Psalms 35:25) 
Judge me according to your righteousness, O Lord my God, and let them not rejoice over me.

(Psalms 35:26) 
Do not let them say in their hearts, “Aha, our hearts’ desire!” Nor let them say, “We have swallowed him up.”

(Psalms 35:27) 
Let those who rejoice at my misfortune be ashamed and disgraced; let those who boast against me be clothed with shame and dishonor.

(Psalms 35:28) 
Let those who desire my vindication shout for joy and be glad; and let them say continually, “The Lord be magnified, who delights in the peace of His servant.”

(Psalms 35:29) 
And my tongue will meditate on your righteousness and your praise all day long.

(Psalms 36:1) 
How long, O Lord, will you completely forget me? How long will you turn your face away from me?

(Psalms 36:2) 
How long will I be forced to consider my anguish in my soul, and my pain in my heart every day?

(Psalms 36:3) 
How long will my enemy have power over me? Consider this, and hear me, O Lord my God.

(Psalms 36:4) 
Enlighten my eyes. Do not ever let me sleep the sleep of death. Otherwise, my enemy will be able to say, 'I have prevailed against him.'

(Psalms 36:5) 
Those who afflict me will rejoice if I am moved and fall. But I have put my hope in your mercy.

(Psalms 36:6) 
My heart will rejoice at your salvation. I will sing to the Lord, because He has given me good things.

(Psalms 36:7) 
The Lord will reward me according to my righteousness, and according to the purity of my hands in his sight.

(Psalms 36:8) 
Because I have kept the ways of the Lord, and I have not acted wickedly against my God.

(Psalms 36:9) 
Because all his judgments are before me; and I have not rejected his justifications.

(Psalms 36:10) 
And I will be blameless with Him; and I will keep myself from sin.

(Psalms 36:11) 
And the Lord will reward me according to my righteousness, and according to the purity of my hands in his sight.

(Psalms 36:12) 
You will be holy with the holy, and innocent with the innocent man.

(Psalms 36:13) 
And you will be chosen with the chosen, and with the perverse, you will be perverse.

(Psalms 36:14) 
For you will save a humble people, and you will bring down the eyes of the proud.

(Psalms 36:15) 
For you will light my lamp, O Lord my God; illuminate my darkness.

(Psalms 36:16) 
For I will be rescued from the temptation in you, and in my God I will cross over the wall.

(Psalms 36:17) 
God's way is immaculate. The words of the Lord are tested by fire; He is the protector of all who hope in Him.

(Psalms 36:18) 
Who is God besides the Lord? Or who is God except our God?

(Psalms 36:19) 
God, who has armed me with virtue, and has made my way immaculate.

(Psalms 36:20) 
Who has made my feet like the feet of the deer, and has established me on high places.

(Psalms 36:21) 
Who teaches my hands for battle, and you have made my arms like a bronze bow.

(Psalms 36:22) 
And you have given me the protection of your salvation; and your right hand has sustained me. Your discipline has corrected me to the end; and your discipline has taught me.

(Psalms 36:23) 
You have enlarged my steps beneath me, and my footsteps have not weakened.

(Psalms 36:24) 
I will pursue my enemies and I will comprehend them; and I will not turn back until they are finished.

(Psalms 36:25) 
I will shatter them, and they will not be able to stand; they will fall beneath my feet.

(Psalms 36:26) 
And you have girded me with virtue for battle; and you have made those who rise against me to stumble.

(Psalms 36:27) 
And you have given my enemies their backs to me, and you have destroyed those who hate me.

(Psalms 36:28) 
They cried out, and there was no one to save them; to the Lord, and he did not hear them.

(Psalms 36:29) 
And I will crush them like dust before the face of the wind. I will trample them like the mud of the streets.

(Psalms 36:30) 
You will rescue me from the contradictions of the people; you will establish me as the head of the Gentiles.

(Psalms 36:31) 
A people I do not know has served me; at the hearing of the ear, they have obeyed me.

(Psalms 36:32) 
Foreign children have lied to me; foreign children have grown old, and they have faltered from their paths.

(Psalms 36:33) 
The Lord lives, and blessed is my God, and let the God of my salvation be exalted.

(Psalms 36:34) 
God, who gives me vengeance, and subjects the peoples under me.

(Psalms 36:35) 
My liberator from my wrathful enemies. You will exalt me from those who rise up against me; you will rescue me from the wicked man.

(Psalms 36:36) 
Therefore, I will confess to you among the Gentiles, O Lord; and I will sing a psalm to your name.

(Psalms 36:37) 
Magnifying the saving acts of his King, and showing mercy to his Christ, David, and to his seed forever.

(Psalms 37:1) 
Don't be jealous of evildoers or those who make a habit of doing what is evil.

(Psalms 37:2) 
Their success is brief like grass—it quickly dries up. They are like all those plants that quickly die.

(Psalms 37:3) 
Trust in the Lord and be good; remain on the land, and He will nourish your soul.

(Psalms 37:4) 
Find joy in the Lord, and He will grant what you ask for.

(Psalms 37:5) 
Entrust your way to the Lord; trust in Him, and He will act.

(Psalms 37:6) 
He will cause your justice to shine like light and your judgment like the midday sun.

(Psalms 37:7) 
Submit to the Lord and pray to Him. Don't be jealous of those who succeed through their own means or of people who do wrong.

(Psalms 37:8) 
Refrain from anger, and abandon fury; don't be jealous and resort to evil.

(Psalms 37:9) 
Because those who do evil will be destroyed, but those who trust in the Lord will inherit the land.

(Psalms 37:10) 
Yet a little while, and the sinner will be no more; you will search for him, but you will not find him.

(Psalms 37:11) 
But the meek will inherit the land and will delight in the abundance of peace.

(Psalms 37:12) 
The sinner plots against the righteous and gnashes his teeth at him.

(Psalms 37:13) 
But the Lord will laugh at him because He sees that his day is coming.

(Psalms 37:14) 
The sinners have drawn their sword and bent their bow to strike the poor and needy, to slaughter the upright of heart.

(Psalms 37:15) 
Let their sword enter their own hearts, and let their bow be broken.

(Psalms 37:16) 
Better is a little that the righteous has than the great wealth of the wicked.

(Psalms 37:17) 
Because the arms of the sinners will be broken, but the Lord upholds the righteous.

(Psalms 37:18) 
The Lord knows the days of the blameless, and their inheritance will be eternal.

(Psalms 37:19) 
They will not be ashamed in the time of evil, and in the days of famine they will be satisfied; because the wicked will be consumed.

(Psalms 37:20) 
For the enemies of the Lord, though they may be honored and exalted, will vanish like smoke.

(Psalms 37:21) 
The sinner borrows but does not pay back, but the righteous shows mercy and gives.

(Psalms 37:22) 
For those whom He blesses will inherit the land, but those whom He curses will perish.

(Psalms 37:23) 
The steps of a man are directed by the Lord, and when He desires his way, He makes it wide.

(Psalms 37:24) 
Though he falls, he will not be crushed, because the Lord sustains him with His hand.

(Psalms 37:25) 
I was young and now I am old, and I have not seen the righteous forsaken or his children begging for bread.

(Psalms 37:26) 
All day long, the righteous shows mercy and lends, and his seed will be a blessing.

(Psalms 37:27) 
Turn away from evil and do good, and remain forever.

(Psalms 37:28) 
Because the Lord loves justice and will not forsake His saints; they will be preserved forever.

(Psalms 37:29) 
The wicked will be punished, and the seed of the impious will perish.

(Psalms 37:30) 
But the righteous will inherit the land and will dwell on it forever.

(Psalms 37:31) 
The mouth of the righteous utters wisdom, and his tongue speaks of justice.

(Psalms 37:32) 
The law of his God is in his heart, and his steps will not be tripped up.

(Psalms 37:33) 
The sinner watches the righteous and seeks to kill him.

(Psalms 37:34) 
But the Lord will not leave him in his hands nor condemn him when he is judged.

(Psalms 37:35) 
Wait for the Lord and keep His way, and He will exalt you to inherit the land; you will see when the sinners are destroyed.

(Psalms 37:36) 
I have seen the wicked exalted and lifted up like the cedars of Lebanon.

(Psalms 37:37) 
Then I passed by, and behold, he was gone; I searched for him, but his place could not be found.

(Psalms 37:38) 
Guard innocence and look to integrity, because there is a future for the man of peace.

(Psalms 37:39) 
But the wicked will perish together, and the future of the impious will be destroyed.

(Psalms 37:40) 
But the salvation of the righteous comes from the Lord, and He is their protector in the time of tribulation.

(Psalms 37:41) 
And the Lord will help them and deliver them; He will rescue them from the sinners and save them, because they have hoped in Him.

(Psalms 38:1) 
Lord, do not rebuke me in your anger, nor correct me in your wrath.

(Psalms 38:2) 
Because your arrows have struck me, and your hand has pressed down upon me.

(Psalms 38:3) 
My body is in pain because of your anger, and my bones have no rest because of my sins.

(Psalms 38:4) 
My sins have overwhelmed me; they are a heavy burden, too heavy for me to bear.

(Psalms 38:5) 
My wounds are foul and festering because of my foolishness.

(Psalms 38:6) 
I am bowed down and brought low; all day long I go about mourning.

(Psalms 38:7) 
My loins are filled with fever, and there is no health in my body.

(Psalms 38:8) 
I am feeble and utterly crushed; I groan because of the anguish of my heart.

(Psalms 38:9) 
Lord, all my longing is before you; my sighing is not hidden from you.

(Psalms 38:10) 
My heart pounds, my strength fails me; even the light of my eyes is gone from me.

(Psalms 38:11) 
My friends and companions avoid me because of my affliction; my neighbors stand far off.

(Psalms 38:12) 
Those who seek my life set traps for me, those who want to harm me speak of ruin and meditate treachery all day long.

(Psalms 38:13) 
But I, like the deaf, do not hear; I am like the mute, who cannot open his mouth.

(Psalms 38:14) 
I am like one who does not hear, whose mouth cannot offer a retort.

(Psalms 38:15) 
I wait for you, Lord; you will answer, Lord my God.

(Psalms 38:16) 
I said, “Do not let them gloat over me, those who triumph when my foot slips.”

(Psalms 38:17) 
For I am ready to fall, and my pain is ever with me.

(Psalms 38:18) 
I confess my iniquity; I am sorry for my sin.

(Psalms 38:19) 
My enemies are vigorous, and those who hate me without cause are numerous.

(Psalms 38:20) 
Those who repay good with evil, they slander me for pursuing good.

(Psalms 38:21) 
Do not forsake me, Lord; do not be far from me, my God.

(Psalms 38:22) 
Come quickly to help me, O Lord, my Savior.

(Psalms 39:1) 
I said: “I will keep myself from sin, so that I do not sin with my words.” I put a watch over my mouth when wicked men were present, speaking against me.

(Psalms 39:2) 
I was silent, and humbled myself, and held my tongue, even from doing good. But my pain was renewed.

(Psalms 39:3) 
My heart grew hot within me, and in my meditation, a fire blazed up.

(Psalms 39:4) 
I spoke then with my tongue: “Show me, Lord, what is my end, and what is the number of my days, so that I might know what I truly lack.”

(Psalms 39:5) 
Behold, you have measured out my days, and my substance is as nothing before you. Yes, every man living is mere vanity.

(Psalms 39:6) 
Truly, man walks about as a shadow, and he is troubled in vain. He gathers riches but doesn't know who will possess them.

(Psalms 39:7) 
And now, what is my expectation? Is it not the Lord? And my hope is in you.

(Psalms 39:8) 
Deliver me from all my iniquities. Do not make me a disgrace to the foolish.

(Psalms 39:9) 
I was silent and did not open my mouth, because you have done this.

(Psalms 39:10) 
Remove your plagues from me. I am worn out by the power of your hand.

(Psalms 39:11) 
With rebuke, you have corrected man for iniquity. And like a moth, you have made his soul waste away. Yet, every man is but vanity.

(Psalms 39:12) 
Hear my prayer, Lord, and heed my supplication. Give ear to my tears. Do not be silent, for I am a stranger before you and a pilgrim like all my fathers.

(Psalms 39:13) 
Forgive me, that I may be refreshed before I go away and be seen no more.

(Psalms 40:1) 
I waited and waited on the Lord, and He turned to me.

(Psalms 40:2) 
He heard my prayers and took me out of the pit of misery and the mud of the swamp.

(Psalms 40:3) 
He set my feet on solid ground, and made my steps sure.

(Psalms 40:4) 
He put a new song in my mouth, a hymn to our God.

(Psalms 40:5) 
Many will see and be afraid, and then they will trust in the Lord.

(Psalms 40:6) 
Blessed is the man whose trust is in the Lord, and who has not looked at vanity and false madness.

(Psalms 40:7) 
O Lord my God, You have done many wonderful things, and no one can match Your thoughts.

(Psalms 40:8) 
I have proclaimed them, and spoken them, and they have multiplied beyond number.

(Psalms 40:9) 
You didn't want sacrifices or offerings; rather, you have perfected my ears.

(Psalms 40:10) 
You didn't ask for burnt offerings or sacrifices for sin, so I said, “Behold, I come.”

(Psalms 40:11) 
It is written of me in the book: “I want to do Your will, O my God, and Your law is within my heart.”

(Psalms 40:12) 
I have proclaimed Your justice in the great assembly; behold, I do not restrain my lips; O Lord, You know this.

(Psalms 40:13) 
I have not hidden Your justice in my heart; I have proclaimed Your truth and Your salvation.

(Psalms 40:14) 
I have not concealed Your mercy and Your truth from the great multitude.

(Psalms 40:15) 
Don’t withhold Your mercy from me, O Lord; Your mercy and truth have always protected me.

(Psalms 40:16) 
For evils without number have surrounded me; my sins have overtaken me, and I can’t see a way out.

(Psalms 40:17) 
They are more than the hairs on my head, those who hate me without cause.

(Psalms 40:18) 
Those who persecute me are strengthened, my unjust enemies; I was made to pay for what I did not steal.

(Psalms 40:19) 
O God, don’t be far from me; my God, look upon me to help me.

(Psalms 40:20) 
Let them be ashamed and disgraced, all who seek my life to take it away.

(Psalms 40:21) 
Let those who wish me evil turn back and be ashamed.

(Psalms 40:22) 
Let them be brought to immediate shame, those who say to me, “Well done, well done!”

(Psalms 40:23) 
Let all who seek You rejoice and be glad in You; and let those who love Your salvation always say, “May the Lord be glorified!”

(Psalms 40:24) 
But I am poor and needy; the Lord cares for me.

(Psalms 40:25) 
You are my helper and my protector; O my God, don’t delay.

(Psalms 41:1) 
To the end, for David, in memory.

(Psalms 41:2) 
Happy is the person who cares for the needy. In the day of evil, the Lord will free him.

(Psalms 41:3) 
May the Lord preserve him, and may the Lord make him live. May He bless him upon the earth, and may He not give him over to the will of his enemies.

(Psalms 41:4) 
May the Lord assist him on his bed of suffering. You have turned over the entire bed for him in his weakness.

(Psalms 41:5) 
I said, "Lord, have mercy on me; heal my soul, because I have sinned against You."

(Psalms 41:6) 
My enemies spoke evil against me. "When will he die, and when will his name perish?"

(Psalms 41:7) 
And if he was entering to see me, he spoke in vain. His heart gathered iniquity for himself.

(Psalms 41:8) 
He was cast out, and he spoke in the same way.

(Psalms 41:9) 
All my enemies whispered against me. They were thinking up evil against me.

(Psalms 41:10) 
They have planned an unjust word against me. "Does he who is sleeping not add to rise again?"

(Psalms 41:11) 
For even the man of my peace, in whom I hoped, who ate my bread, greatly lifted his heel against me.

(Psalms 41:12) 
But You, Lord, have mercy on me, and raise me up that I may repay them.

(Psalms 41:13) 
By this, I have known that You have wanted me, because my enemy will not rejoice over me.

(Psalms 41:14) 
But You have upheld me because of my innocence, and You have confirmed me in Your sight forever.

(Psalms 41:15) 
Blessed be the Lord, the God of Israel, from all eternity to eternity. So be it, so be it.

(Psalms 42:1) 
Like a deer thirsting for water, my soul thirsts for You, O God.

(Psalms 42:2) 
My soul thirsts for the living God;

(Psalms 42:3) 
When will I come and appear before the face of God?

(Psalms 42:4) 
My tears have been my bread day and night, while they say to me daily: "Where is your God?"

(Psalms 42:5) 
I remember these things, and I pour out my soul within me:

(Psalms 42:6) 
How I used to walk in the temple, as if to the house of God, among the sound of joy and thanksgiving, with a crowd celebrating a feast.

(Psalms 42:7) 
Why are you sad, my soul? And why do you disquiet me?

(Psalms 42:8) 
Hope in God, for I will still give praise to Him, the saving presence of my countenance.

(Psalms 42:9) 
My God, my soul is troubled within me; therefore I will remember you from the land of the Jordan and of Hermon and from the little mountain.

(Psalms 42:10) 
Deep calls to deep at the noise of your waterfalls;

(Psalms 42:11) 
all your exalted waves and your billows have passed over me.

(Psalms 42:12) 
By day the Lord commands his mercy, and at night his song.

(Psalms 42:13) 
Let my prayer go to the God of my life, and I will say:

(Psalms 42:14) 
“Why have you forgotten me? Why do I go about sad, while the enemy afflicts me?”

(Psalms 42:15) 
As my bones are broken, the enemies who afflict me have reproached me.

(Psalms 42:16) 
As they say to me daily: "Where is your God?"

(Psalms 42:17) 
Why are you sad, my soul? And why do you disquiet me?

(Psalms 42:18) 
Hope in God, for I will still give praise to Him, my salvation, and my God.

(Psalms 43:1) 
Give me justice, O God, and defend my cause from a nation that isn’t holy. Deliver me from the hands of wicked and deceitful people.

(Psalms 43:2) 
For You are the God who protects me: why have you rejected me? Why do I walk around so sad and downtrodden when my enemies are constantly bothering me?

(Psalms 43:3) 
Send forth Your light and Your truth. Those things have guided me, and lead me back up to your holy mountain, and to Your tabernacles.

(Psalms 43:4) 
Then I will go to the altar of God: to God, who gives joy to my youth.

(Psalms 43:5) 
I will give thanks to You with a harp, O God, my God. Why are you sad, my soul? Why do you disturb me?

(Psalms 43:6) 
Hope in God, because I will still give Him thanks. He is the salvation of my face, and He is my God.

(Psalms 44:1) 
For the leader. A song for the sons of Korah, a prayer for understanding.

(Psalms 44:2) 
Listen to this, all you nations. Understand this, all who live on Earth.

(Psalms 44:3) 
Consider this, you who are of the earth, and all the sons of men. Both rich and poor come together, for all are equal.

(Psalms 44:4) 
My mouth will speak wisdom, and my heart will ponder prudence.

(Psalms 44:5) 
I will listen closely to a parable. I will solve the mystery by singing a song.

(Psalms 44:6) 
Why should I fear trouble? The wickedness of my life seeks to surround me.

(Psalms 44:7) 
They trust in their own strength, and boast in the abundance of their riches.

(Psalms 44:8) 
No man can pay the price to save a brother. Man cannot give God the price of redemption.

(Psalms 44:9) 
For he cannot pay to satisfy God's justice, nor give enough to save his own soul.

(Psalms 44:10) 
For he will labor forever, and continue to live in his misery without end.

(Psalms 44:11) 
He will not see corruption, when he sees wise men dying. The fool and the stupid will perish together.

(Psalms 44:12) 
And they leave their riches to others.

(Psalms 44:13) 
Their tombs will be their houses forever. Their dwellings will be from generation to generation.

(Psalms 44:14) 
They have given names to the lands which they possess.

(Psalms 44:15) 
But man, though living in honor, does not understand. He is compared to unthinking beasts, and becomes like them.

(Psalms 44:16) 
This is the way of them that cause trouble. Their mouths approve of their own wickedness.

(Psalms 44:17) 
Like sheep in the grave, death will feed on them.

(Psalms 44:18) 
The just shall rule over them at the resurrection, and their strength will waste away in the grave, far from their glory.

(Psalms 44:19) 
But God will redeem my soul from the power of hell, for He will receive me.

(Psalms 44:20) 
Do not fear when a man becomes rich, or when the glory of his house is increased.

(Psalms 44:21) 
For when he dies, he will take nothing. His glory will not follow him down.

(Psalms 44:22) 
Because his soul, while he lives, is blessed. He will give thanks to You when You bless him.

(Psalms 44:23) 
He will go to the generation of his fathers. And he will never again see the light.

(Psalms 44:24) 
Man, while living in honor, does not understand. He is compared to unthinking beasts, and becomes like them.

(Psalms 45:1) 
My heart swells with a message from God. I will write my poem to the King.

(Psalms 45:2) 
My tongue will be like the ready pen of a skilled writer.

(Psalms 45:3) 
You are the fairest of all men. Grace is poured out on your lips, and God has blessed you forever.

(Psalms 45:4) 
Gird your sword upon your thigh, O mighty one.

(Psalms 45:5) 
In your glory and your beauty, ride forth, and reign.

(Psalms 45:6) 
Ride forth for truth, gentleness, and righteousness. Let your right hand perform awesome deeds.

(Psalms 45:7) 
Your arrows are sharp, and nations will fall before you, piercing the hearts of the king's enemies.

(Psalms 45:8) 
Your throne, O God, is forever and ever; a scepter of justice is the scepter of your kingdom.

(Psalms 45:9) 
You love justice and hate wickedness; therefore, God, your God, has anointed you with the oil of gladness above your fellows.

(Psalms 45:10) 
Your robes are fragrant with myrrh, aloes, and cassia; from the ivory palaces, stringed instruments make you rejoice.

(Psalms 45:11) 
Daughters of kings are among those held in honor; the queen stands at your right hand, adorned with gold from Ophir.

(Psalms 45:12) 
Hear, O daughter, consider and incline your ear: forget your people and your father's house.

(Psalms 45:13) 
And the king will desire your beauty; he is your lord, and you shall bow down to him.

(Psalms 45:14) 
The people of Tyre will seek your favor with gifts; the rich among the people will seek your blessing.

(Psalms 45:15) 
All glorious is the princess within; her gown is woven with gold.

(Psalms 45:16) 
In embroidered garments she is led to the king; after her the virgins, her companions, are brought to you.

(Psalms 45:17) 
They are led forth with gladness and rejoicing; they enter the palace of the king.

(Psalms 45:18) 
Your sons will take the place of your fathers; you will make them princes throughout all the earth.

(Psalms 45:19) 
I will cause your name to be remembered in all generations;

(Psalms 45:20) 
therefore the peoples will praise you forever and ever.

(Psalms 46:1) 
A song for the liturgical use of the sons of Korah, for the soul.

(Psalms 46:2) 
God is our safe-haven and His power is our strength. He is the help we need during the tribulations that have found us.

(Psalms 46:3) 
Therefore, we will not fear even when the earth is shaken. Even if the mountains are moved into the depths of the sea...

(Psalms 46:4) 
Their waters have roared and foamed over; the mountains have trembled and been disturbed by His strength.

(Psalms 46:5) 
The rush of the river brings joy to the city of God. The Most High sanctified His tabernacle.

(Psalms 46:6) 
God is in the midst of the city, and it will not be moved. God will help it, even at the break of dawn.

(Psalms 46:7) 
The nations were troubled and the kingdoms were inclined. God spoke, and the earth was moved.

(Psalms 46:8) 
The Lord of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our protector.

(Psalms 46:9) 
Come and see the works of the Lord, the amazing things He has done on Earth.

(Psalms 46:10) 
He stops wars all over the Earth. He breaks the bow, shatters the spear, and burns the shields in the fire.

(Psalms 46:11) 
Be still, and know that I am God; I will be exalted among the nations, and I will be exalted in the earth.

(Psalms 46:12) 
The Lord of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our protector.

(Psalms 48:1) 
A song of the psalms, for the sons of Korah. The Lord is great, and worthy of all praise: in the city of our God, on his holy mountain.

(Psalms 48:2) 
It is beautiful, the joy of all the earth, Mount Zion, and the sides of the north, the city of the great King.

(Psalms 48:3) 
God is known in His houses, when He shall take her.

(Psalms 48:4) 
For, behold, the kings of the earth are gathered: they have come together.

(Psalms 48:5) 
They saw, and so they marveled; they were troubled, they were moved.

(Psalms 48:6) 
Trembling took hold of them: there were pains like a woman in labor.

(Psalms 48:7) 
With a strong wind, You will break the ships of Tarshish.

(Psalms 48:8) 
As we have heard, so have we seen: in the city of the Lord of hosts, in the city of our God: God has founded her forever.

(Psalms 48:9) 
We have received, O God, Your mercy, in the midst of You.

(Psalms 48:10) 
According to Your name, O God, so also is Your praise to the ends of the earth: Your right hand is full of justice.

(Psalms 48:11)

(Psalms 48:12)

(Psalms 48:13)
