“Lord, deliver my soul!” For the Lord is merciful, just, and our God is full of mercy.

The Lord protects the simple. I was humbled, and He saved me.

(Psalms 116:7)

(Psalms 116:8) 
For He has delivered my soul from death, my eyes from tears, and my feet from stumbling.

I will walk before the Lord in the land of the living.

(Psalms 116:11)

(Psalms 123:1) 
A Song of Ascents. Unless the Lord builds a home, the builders labor in vain. Unless the Lord protects the city, the watchman guards it in vain.

(Psalms 123:2) 
It is useless to wake up before dawn. You who work so hard to earn a living, you will still be left with little.

(Psalms 123:3) 
For those who trust in God, He gives rest. Behold, sons are a heritage from the Lord, the reward of the fruit of the womb.

(Psalms 123:4) 
As arrows are in the hand of a warrior, so are the children of one's youth.

(Psalms 123:5) 
Happy is the man who has filled his quiver with them. They will not be ashamed when they fight against their enemies in the gates of the city.

(Psalms 124:1) 
A Song of Ascents. If the Lord hadn't been on our side—let Israel say so:

(Psalms 124:2) 
If the Lord hadn't been on our side when men rose up against us,

(Psalms 124:3) 
they would have swallowed us alive when their fury blazed against us.

(Psalms 124:4) 
The flood waters might have drowned us.

(Psalms 124:5) 
The torrent of their anger surged over our souls.

(Psalms 124:6) 
We might have been swept away by an intolerable flood.

(Psalms 124:7) 
Blessed be the Lord, who didn't give us as prey to their teeth.

(Psalms 124:8) 
We escaped like a bird from the fowler’s snare.

(Psalms 124:9) 
The snare was broken, and we were freed.

(Psalms 124:10) 
Our help is in the name of the Lord, who made the universe and the earth.

(Psalms 125:3)

(Psalms 125:4)

(Psalms 125:5)

By the rivers of Babylon, we sat and wept when we remembered Zion.

We hung our instruments of music in the willows there.

(Psalms 137:3) 
For there, those who had taken us captive asked for a song, and those who had led us away asked for a hymn.

(Psalms 137:4) 
Sing us one of the songs of Zion!

(Psalms 137:5) 
How can we sing the Lord's song in a foreign land?

(Psalms 137:6) 
If I forget you, Jerusalem, may my right hand be forgotten!

(Psalms 137:7) 
If I do not remember you, if I do not prefer Jerusalem above my chief joy...

(Psalms 137:8)

(Psalms 138:1) 
Lord, you put me to the test, and I know that you know me.

(Psalms 138:2) 
You know when I sit down, and when I stand up;

(Psalms 138:3) 
You read my thoughts from afar.

(Psalms 138:4) 
You have surveyed my path and my journey;

(Psalms 138:5) 
and you have foreseen all my ways.

(Psalms 138:6) 
Because before the words come out of my mouth, you know them completely, Lord.

(Psalms 138:7) 
You formed me from the very beginning, and you have always been present.

(Psalms 138:8) 
This is a great wonder to me;

(Psalms 138:9) 
it is so powerful, and I can't begin to comprehend it.

(Psalms 138:10) 
Where can I go to escape your spirit? Where can I flee from your face?

(Psalms 138:11) 
If I ascend into the sky, you are there;

(Psalms 138:12) 
if I go down to hell, you are there.

(Psalms 138:13) 
If I fly to the ends of the earth and take wings in the morning,

(Psalms 138:14) 
even there your hand will lead me, and your right hand will hold me.

(Psalms 138:15) 
And I said, "Surely darkness will conceal me;"

(Psalms 138:16) 
and night will be my light in my pleasure.

(Psalms 138:17) 
Even darkness isn't dark to you, and night is as bright as the day: both the darkness and the light are the same to you.

(Psalms 138:18) 
For you have made me;

(Psalms 138:19) 
you have received me in my mother's womb.

(Psalms 138:20) 
I will praise you, because you are a wonderful, amazing God;

(Psalms 138:21) 
your works are miraculous, and my soul knows this well.

(Psalms 138:22) 
My body was not hidden from you when I was being formed secretly;

(Psalms 138:23) 
and all parts of my body were being made in the depths of the earth.

(Psalms 138:24) 
Your eyes saw my imperfection, and in your book all things were written;

(Psalms 138:25) 
the days of my life have been formed, and not one of them is without you.

(Psalms 138:26) 
And how precious to me are your friends, O God! How powerful are their leaders!

(Psalms 138:27) 
I will count them, and they will increase more than the sand: if I rise up, I am still with you.

(Psalms 138:28) 
If you slay the wicked, God, men of bloodshed, get away from me:

(Psalms 138:29) 
because they speak deceitfully and take your cities in vain.

(Psalms 138:31)

(Psalms 138:32)

(Psalms 138:33)

O Lord, you have examined me, and you have known me.

(Psalms 139:6) 
Behold, O Lord, you have known all things new and old.

(Psalms 139:7) 
You have made me, and put your hand upon me.

(Psalms 139:8) 
Your knowledge has become wonderful and mysterious, and I cannot attain it.

(Psalms 139:9)

(Psalms 139:10) 
If I go up into the sky, you are there. If I go down into the underworld, you are there.

(Psalms 139:12) 
Even there your hand will lead me, and your right hand will hold me.

(Psalms 139:13) 
And if I say: Perhaps the darkness will overwhelm me: and night will be my illumination in my delights:

(Psalms 139:14) 
Even the darkness will not be hidden from you, and night will be illuminated like day. As is its darkness, so is its light.

(Psalms 139:15) 
For you have possessed my kidneys: you have taken me from my mother's womb.

(Psalms 139:16) 
I will give you praise: because you have been fearfully magnified. Wonderful are your works, and my soul knows this exceedingly well.

(Psalms 139:17) 
My bone was not hidden from you, that you have made in secret: and my substance in the lower parts of the earth.

(Psalms 139:18) 
Your eyes have seen my imperfection, and in your book all are written: days will be formed, and there will be none among them.

(Psalms 139:19) 
But to me, your friends are greatly honored, O God: their leadership is greatly strengthened.

(Psalms 139:20) 
I will count them, and they will be multiplied above the sand: I have risen, and I am still with you.

(Psalms 139:21) 
If, O God, you will kill the sinners: men of blood, seek blood from me.

(Psalms 139:22) 
Who say in thought: We will take your cities in vain.

(Psalms 139:23) 
Do I not hate those who hate you, O Lord? And do I not waste away because of your enemies?

(Psalms 139:24) 
I hated them with a perfect hatred: they have become my enemies.

(Psalms 139:25) 
Test me, O God, and know my heart: question me, and know my ways.

(Psalms 139:26) 
And see if the way of iniquity is in me: and lead me in the way everlasting.

(Psalms 140:1) 
For the leader. A psalm of David.

(Psalms 140:2) 
Lord, I cried to you. Hear me. Pay attention to my voice when I cry out to you.

(Psalms 140:3) 
May my prayer rise before you like incense. May my hands lifted up be a sacrifice in the evening.

(Psalms 140:4) 
O Lord, set a guard over my mouth. And keep watch at the door of my lips.

(Psalms 140:5) 
Do not turn my heart to the words of evil. Do not let me make excuses for my sins.

(Psalms 140:6) 
Do not let me make excuses with those who do evil, nor should I befriend those who are evil.

(Psalms 140:7) 
Let the righteous correct me with mercy, and rebuke me. But the oil of a sinner should not make my head fat.

(Psalms 140:8) 
Because my prayer is always their will. Their judges are completely destroyed by their sins.

(Psalms 140:9) 
They will hear my words and understand that they could not resist my prayer, as the very earth cracked open. Their bones are scattered according to the grave.

(Psalms 140:10) 
Because my eyes are turned towards you, O Lord. I have put my trust in you. Do not take away my soul.

(Psalms 140:11) 
Keep me from the trap they have set for me, and from the snares of those who do evil.

(Psalms 140:12) 
The wicked will fall into their own net. Meanwhile, I am alone until I pass through their traps.

(Psalms 141:1) 
Lord, I am calling to You. Answer me. Listen to my voice as I call to You.

(Psalms 141:2) 
Let my prayer be as incense in Your sight, and the lifting up of my hands be as the evening sacrifice.

(Psalms 141:3) 
Set a guard, Lord, over my mouth, and a door to enclose my lips.

(Psalms 141:4) 
Do not incline my heart to words of evil or to the making of excuses for sin.

(Psalms 141:5) 
Let me not take part in the works of the evildoers. May I not be numbered among them.

(Psalms 141:6) 
The just man will strike me with mercy and will rebuke me. But the oil of the sinner will not anoint my head.

(Psalms 141:7) 
For even in their evil prayers, their judges have been swallowed up in the rock.

(Psalms 141:8) 
My words are heard for they have prevailed. Like the earth, they are upon the earth. Their bones are scattered near hell.

(Psalms 141:9) 
For my eyes are turned to You, Lord. I have hoped in You, do not take away my soul.

(Psalms 141:10) 
Keep me from the snare that they have laid for me, and from the snares of those who do evil.

(Psalms 141:11) 
The sinners will fall in the net that they made for themselves. I will be alone until I pass by.

(Psalms 142:1) 
A Psalm of David. Lord, hear my prayer; listen to my plea, and fulfill it. Respond to my prayer in truth, and hear my plea in your justice.

(Psalms 142:2) 
Do not enter into judgment with your servant, because no living thing will be just by your standards.

(Psalms 142:3) 
My enemy has hounded my soul and humiliated my life in this world.

(Psalms 142:4) 
I am placed in the darkness, among those in the grave. My spirit is anxious, my heart is troubled.

(Psalms 142:5) 
I recall the days of old, I reflect on all your works, and I meditate on what your hands have made.

(Psalms 142:6) 
I stretch out my hands to you; my soul is like a barren land yearning for you.

(Psalms 142:7) 
Answer me quickly, Lord; my spirit fails.

(Psalms 142:8) 
Do not turn your face away from me, lest I be like those who go down to the pit.

(Psalms 142:9) 
Let me hear your kindness in the morning, for I trust in you.

(Psalms 142:10) 
Show me the way I should go, for I lift up my soul to you.

(Psalms 142:11) 
Rescue me from my enemies, Lord; I flee to you for refuge.

(Psalms 142:12) 
Teach me to do your will, for you are my God.

(Psalms 142:13) 
Your good Spirit will lead me on the right path; for the sake of your name, revive me.

(Psalms 142:14) 
In your justice, bring my soul out of trouble.

(Psalms 142:15) 
In your mercy, destroy my enemies and destroy all who harass my soul, for I am your servant.

(Psalms 143:1) 
A psalm of David. Lord, listen to my prayer. Hear my plea in your truth. Listen to me in your righteousness.

(Psalms 143:2) 
Do not punish me with a judgment because no person can be made just by God.

(Psalms 143:3) 
The enemy has hunted my soul, and has crushed my life.

(Psalms 143:4) 
He has put me into darkness, like those who are in the grave. My spirit has grown faint. My heart is troubled within me.

(Psalms 143:5) 
I remember the ancient days; I reflect on all your works, and I meditate on your achievements.

(Psalms 143:6) 
I stretch out my hands to you; my soul is like land that thirsts for your presence.

(Psalms 143:7) 
Answer me quickly, Lord. My spirit fails. Do not turn your face away from me, or I will be like those who go down into the pit.

(Psalms 143:8) 
Let me hear of your loving kindness in the morning because I put my trust in you. Show me the way I should go, because to you I lift up my soul.

(Psalms 143:9) 
Deliver me from my enemies, Lord, because I run to you for help. Teach me to do your will because you are my God.

(Psalms 143:10) 
Let your good Spirit lead me into a land of uprightness, and for your name’s sake, give me life.

(Psalms 143:11) 
In your righteousness bring my soul out of trouble. Destroy my enemies in your mercy.

(Psalms 143:12) 
Destroy all those who torment my soul because I am your servant.

(Psalms 144:1) 
I will exalt you, my God, the King, and I will bless your name for all time and forever.

(Psalms 144:2) 
Every day I will bless you, and I will praise your name for all time and forever.

(Psalms 144:3) 
Great is the Lord, and exceedingly praiseworthy, and there is no end to his greatness.

(Psalms 144:4) 
Generation after generation will praise your works, and will announce your power.

(Psalms 144:5) 
They will speak of the magnificence of the glory of your holiness, and they will tell of your wonders.

(Psalms 144:6) 
They will speak of the power of your awesome deeds, and they will narrate your greatness.

(Psalms 144:7) 
They will pour forth the memory of your abundant sweetness and will rejoice in your justice.

(Psalms 144:8) 
The Lord is merciful and compassionate, patient, and of great mercy.

(Psalms 144:9) 
The Lord is good to all, and his mercies are over all his works.

(Psalms 144:10) 
May all your works give thanks to you, O Lord, and may your holy ones bless you.

(Psalms 144:11) 
They will speak of the glory of your kingdom, and they will talk of your power:

(Psalms 144:12) 
so that they may make known to the sons of men your power and the glory of the beauty of your kingdom.

(Psalms 144:13) 
Your kingdom is the kingdom of all ages, and your dominion is in every generation.

(Psalms 144:14) 
The Lord is faithful in all his words, and holy in all his works.

(Psalms 144:15) 
The Lord strengthens all who are falling, and raises up all who are bowed down.

(Psalms 144:16) 
The eyes of all hope in you, O Lord, and you give them food in due season.

(Psalms 144:17) 
You open your hand and fill every living thing with blessing.

(Psalms 144:18) 
The Lord is just in all his ways, and holy in all his works.

(Psalms 144:19) 
The Lord is near to all who call upon him, to all who call upon him in truth.

(Psalms 144:20) 
He will fulfill the desire of those who fear him, and he will hear their prayer and save them.

(Psalms 144:21) 
The Lord protects all who love him, but he will destroy all the wicked.

(Psalms 144:22) 
My mouth will speak the praise of the Lord, and let all flesh bless his holy name for all time and forever.

(Psalms 145:1) 
I will praise you, my God, and King. I will give thanks to your name forever and ever.

(Psalms 145:2) 
Every single day I will bless you. I will praise your name forever and ever.

(Psalms 145:3) 
The Lord is great, and praiseworthy above all things. His greatness has no end.

(Psalms 145:4) 
Each generation will praise your works. They will declare your power.

(Psalms 145:5) 
They will speak of the magnificence of your holy glory and will tell of your wondrous deeds.

(Psalms 145:6) 
They will declare the power of your terrifying works and tell of your greatness.

(Psalms 145:7) 
They will burst forth with the memory of your abundant goodness and rejoice in your justice.

(Psalms 145:8) 
The Lord is merciful and kind, patient, and of great mercy.

(Psalms 145:9) 
The Lord is sweet to all. His mercy is over all his works.

(Psalms 145:10) 
All your works, O Lord, will give thanks to you, and your holy ones will bless you.

(Psalms 145:11) 
They will declare the glory of your kingdom and speak of your power,

(Psalms 145:12) 
to make known to the sons of men your power and the glorious splendor of your kingdom.

(Psalms 145:13) 
Your kingdom is a kingdom of all ages. Your dominion endures through all generations.

(Psalms 145:14) 
The Lord is faithful in all His words and holy in all His works.

(Psalms 145:15) 
The Lord supports all who fall and raises up all who are bowed down.

(Psalms 145:16) 
The eyes of all look to you, O Lord, and you give them food at the proper time.

(Psalms 145:17) 
You open your hand, and you fill every living thing with blessing.

(Psalms 145:18) 
The Lord is just in all His ways and holy in all His works.

(Psalms 145:19) 
The Lord is near to all who call upon Him, to all who call upon Him in truth.

(Psalms 145:20) 
He will fulfill the will of those who fear Him. He hears their prayer and saves them.

(Psalms 145:21) 
The Lord protects all who love Him, but He will destroy all the wicked.

(Psalms 145:22) 
My mouth will speak the praise of the Lord, and all flesh will bless His holy name forever and ever.

(Psalms 146:1) 
Praise God, because He is good! Sing to our God, because He is full of joy.

(Psalms 146:2) 
God is the one who builds Jerusalem; He will gather all the scattered people of Israel.

(Psalms 146:3) 
He heals those whose hearts are broken, and He binds up their wounds.

(Psalms 146:4) 
He knows the number of the stars and calls each of them by name.

(Psalms 146:5) 
Our Lord is great, and His power is great, and there is no limit to His wisdom.

(Psalms 146:6) 
God supports the gentle. But He humbles sinners down to the earth.

(Psalms 146:7) 
Sing to God, giving thanks; sing to our God with a harp.

(Psalms 146:8) 
He covers the sky with clouds, and He prepares rain for the earth. He makes grass grow on the mountains, and crops for the service of men.

(Psalms 146:9) 
He gives food to the cattle, and to the young ravens when they call to Him.

(Psalms 146:10) 
He does not delight in the strength of the horse, nor does He take pleasure in the legs of a man.

(Psalms 146:11) 
God takes pleasure in those who fear Him, and in those who hope in His mercy.

(Psalms 146:12) 
Praise the Lord, Jerusalem! Praise your God, Zion!

(Psalms 146:13) 
Because He has strengthened the locks of your gates; He has blessed your children within you.

(Psalms 146:14) 
He makes peace in your borders and fills you with the finest wheat.

(Psalms 146:15) 
He sends out His word to the earth; quickly runs His word.

(Psalms 146:16) 
He gives snow like wool, scatters the mist like ashes.

(Psalms 146:17) 
He sends His ice like crumbs; who can stand against His cold?

(Psalms 146:18) 
He sends out His word and melts them; He blows His spirit, and the waters flow.

(Psalms 146:19) 
He declares His word to Jacob, His justice and judgements to Israel.

(Psalms 146:20) 
He has not done this for every nation, and He has not revealed His judgements to them.

(Psalms 147:1) 
Praise God, because He is good. Sing to our God because He is merciful.

(Psalms 147:2) 
God rebuilds Jerusalem; He gathers the scattered people of Israel.

(Psalms 147:3) 
He heals those with broken hearts, and binds up their wounds.

(Psalms 147:4) 
He determines the number of the stars and calls each of them by their name.

(Psalms 147:5) 
Great is our God, and His power is great; His wisdom has no limit.

(Psalms 147:6) 
God helps the poor, but He humbles the wicked and the proud.

(Psalms 147:7) 
Sing to God with thanksgiving, and sing to our God with the harp.

(Psalms 147:8) 
He covers the sky with clouds, provides the rain for the land, makes the grass grow in the mountains, and herbs for human use.

(Psalms 147:9) 
He gives food to the cattle and the young ravens when they call to Him.

(Psalms 147:10) 
He doesn’t take pleasure in the strength of a horse or the speed of a man.

(Psalms 147:11) 
God takes pleasure in those who fear Him and those who hope in His mercy.

(Psalms 147:12) 
Praise God, Jerusalem; Praise your God, Zion.

(Psalms 147:13) 
He strengthens the gates of your city and blesses your children.

(Psalms 147:14) 
He makes peace in your land, and fills you with the finest wheat.

(Psalms 147:15) 
He sends out His word to the earth and His word runs swiftly.

(Psalms 147:16) 
He gives snow like wool; He scatters frost like ashes.

(Psalms 147:17) 
He throws down ice in pieces; who can endure His cold?

(Psalms 147:18) 
He sends out His word, and melts the ice, and when His wind blows, the waters flow.

(Psalms 147:19) 
He proclaims His word to Jacob, His laws and judgments to Israel.

(Psalms 147:20) 
He has not done this for any other nation, and has not revealed His judgments to them. Praise God.

(Psalms 148:1) 
Praise God from the universe! Praise him in the highest heavens.

(Psalms 148:2) 
Praise him, all you angels! Praise him, all the hosts of heaven.

(Psalms 148:3) 
Praise him, sun and moon! Praise him, all the stars and the light they give.

(Psalms 148:4) 
Praise him, highest sky of the heavens! And you waters above the sky, praise the name of God.

(Psalms 148:5) 
Because he spoke, and it was made. He commanded, and everything was created.

(Psalms 148:6) 
He established them for the ages, for all time. He gave a law that cannot be broken.

(Psalms 148:7) 
Praise God from the earth, all dragons and all the deep seas:

(Psalms 148:8) 
Fire, hail, snow, ice, storm winds, all obeying his word:

(Psalms 148:9) 
Mountains and all hills, fruit trees and all cedars:

(Psalms 148:10) 
Wild beasts and all livestock, creeping things and birds:

(Psalms 148:11) 
Kings of the earth and all peoples, princes and all judges of the earth:

(Psalms 148:12) 
Young men and maidens, old men and children, let them all praise God's name:

(Psalms 148:13) 
For his name alone is exalted,

(Psalms 148:14) 
his glory is above the universe and the earth.

(Psalms 148:15) 
He raised up the horn of his people, the song of praise of all his saints, of the children of Israel, the people drawing near to him.

(Psalms 149:1) 
Sing to the Lord a new song, and give praise to him with the congregation of the saints.

(Psalms 149:2) 
Let Israel rejoice that God made them, and let the children of Zion be joyful in their king.

(Psalms 149:3) 
Let them praise his name with dancing, and in musical accompaniment, they shall sing to him.

(Psalms 149:4) 
For God is pleased by his people. He will exalt the humble with salvation.

(Psalms 149:5) 
The saints will exult in glory, and will rejoice on their beds.

(Psalms 149:6) 
Let the praise of God be in their throats, and let them carry the two-edged swords in their hands.

(Psalms 149:7) 
This is to bring vengeance on the nations and punishments on the peoples.

(Psalms 149:8) 
To bind their kings in chains and their nobles in iron shackles.

(Psalms 149:9) 
This is the judgment written for them, and it is the glory that comes to all the saints.

(Psalms 150:1) 
Praise God in his holy place! Praise him in the great universe He created and rules.

(Psalms 150:2) 
Praise Him for the many things He can do! Praise Him because of how great He is!

(Psalms 150:3) 
Praise Him with trumpets! Praise Him with harps and lyres.

(Psalms 150:4) 
Praise Him with drums and in dances! Praise Him with stringed instruments and flutes.

(Psalms 150:5) 
Praise Him with clashing cymbals! Praise Him with loud cymbals! Let everyone and everything with breath praise the Lord!
